* CDL Goal
  The goal of this CDL is for you and your group to think about and discuss what
  you (will have) learned about problem solving from grappling with this variant
  of the Traveling Salesperson Problem (TSP), and relate it to what you have
  already learned about problem solving.


* USA Map with Inter-State-Capital Driving Distances

#+BEGIN_SRC elisp :var distance-table=distance-table
  (list (list 'num-links (length distance-table))
        (list 'num-links-unique-distance (length (remove-duplicates (mapcar 'second distance-table)))))
#+END_SRC


#+BEGIN_SRC elisp :var distance-table=distance-table
  (cl-sort distance-table '< :key 'second)
#+END_SRC

#+BEGIN_SRC elisp :results silent
  (defun get-dist (state1 state2)
    (let ((dist (get state1 state2)))
      (or dist most-positive-fixnum)))
#+END_SRC

#+BEGIN_SRC elisp
  (get-dist 'CA 'WA)
